[30;1m61 | [0m[35mHow to Use the Module[0m
[30;1m62 | [0m[35m=====================[0m
[30;1m63 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m64 | [0m[35mHere is a simple example of how python-crontab is typically used. First the [0m
[30;1m65 | [0m[35mCronTab class is used to instantiate a cron object, then the cron object is used[0m
[30;1m66 | [0m[35mto declaratively manipulate the cron (spawning a new job in this case). Lastly,[0m
[30;1m67 | [0m[35mdeclared changes get written to the crontab by calling write on the object::[0m
[30;1m68 | [0m[35m[0m
